It reduces system performance to lower power consumption [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHM0Jrl8DKTEwbI1HQ5WbkPZlHjHB1TEXqiUYbHxTw1zdCEpZQt4vqEPgiia3__CDrsvzGQB2KySRmlbuwZiNTNDXQEUNEaZguu0GjvKW67ueoqU37XRtRuXLq77oPuRziuTKKkSRtdmdth1QCXYNqiPLk2jzcEEiFoyfg0dXEg0CLXBMtmxgM91) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHT3zammXCQBLHNF9CrWvek9KnbhPavU7HA7DH1iTdd_uIK7PayqpYfW_mE9wRNb1DiIhnKb5j_LQ7d7ZEA8etCHBCIcyfppt3ov_9XFlM1YoB7k8iw3KNBqFXxlDC51FWBxGhPzXkoyinWkJbBV9mkC_hV0lxrCtdnQ5YUvasrjRUwqPD3bSZc9QI1szTt-P7Y-XmwzDEle-mNS53VFc4JAKTpPHWeaQxLs1w=) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHM0Jrl8DKTEwbI1HQ5WbkPZlHjHB1TEXqiUYbHxTw1zdCEpZQt4vqEPgiia3__CDrsvzGQB2KySRmlbuwZiNTNDXQEUNEaZguu0GjvKW67ueoqU37XRtRuXLq77oPuRziuTKKkSRtdmdth1QCXYNqiPLk2jzcEEiFoyfg0dXEg0CLXBMtmxgM92).
    *   **Phone Link:** 24H2 has improvements to phone linking capabilities [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGU8GL3V6_8VitPk8a6EYYZ8p1FSE3FLbfvQIxHv4SRf4BaMU2KCtoczAeIE6V-dP3-U5eqhwlaauW7PJfya2S1-uyFJEZeojGXpUPwm1t-1sHDLJWyo4u_in3mDcdPVFaRUlBwMcZ_F5CR43V-TnncPx-pa24J7n0QLj_aeXFEhtnP3VnKb4aUQR5f9Ix8jb10YD2_IEOMJs5V_oq3SaA0NzXgyLC_zI-CpK49RU1GvO4rW34Je3DBCQ==).
    *   **Other 24H2 Features:** HDR background support [pcmag](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR0), Wi-Fi 7 and Bluetooth LE audio support, improved Windows Search, Auto Super Resolution (on Copilot+ PCs), Windows Recall (preview), and Live Captions for translating audio (Copilot+ PCs) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR1).
    *   **Other 23H2 Features:** New volume mixer [starwindsoftware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR2) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGSCGr69G8mEHDBgXiQqSN_eeJWUG_uY5q9iRMmU3D8gCXtkRhAsK8l76qwekEm9fA_PpTcKGg0NvQ640NCjS0K7Z3KD0FSLdxzeNZiqLGaZT34tJU32xDkprrhHBsT7ybuUD9igpm4nws_VzAfr_BmS16UkTCrsuu4H7ElN3-BzigBP3FovpJYxtajjMwHkVeQSzVIxiJm-vA9MyU-goA4n3yFj4Z9rbAXc5zKjlLge3mTrSZD2itr), Dynamic Lighting and RGB control [starwindsoftware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR2) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFnWZPQJHy1KFAbQcxujWuDs3hMZ9x-lMQrfIqk5vSzeSs-e5__UHEz-lZOLvLuwHQxqFgOu8tC7pL-e1mvaBJfnGsR-aE2R7L1A8kU_xrIfyviC-pPdvSzywOX4HQWP-wwHDA4AtqSIyLUwt8tkmn1xA==), and reintroduced Windows Backup [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQE9e_H2QrXtiOKC0JNteHlVmqyonnp6x3CKoOZ8fGIEE10831BaHPF-5NUfa-PL4klM76BBM6eLiC7_iPk7yS4Pwk8WKAwMdBC5wAKuDHZVH-Bi6NZzyKJtaxpfBBBrkNph_uV0qsDgazhKNPKJbI2-kw==).
*   **System Requirements:** 24H2 requires a x86-64-v2 CPU supporting SSE4.2 and POPCNT CPU instructions [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx2) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF9lBOUpt0Su9Ha8-vwby6EmsuVHPmtgIvokFeAD-oLhOe8skcN-wb-MY2ykmCEpHaqh_8DunqsvH3_tX6jHGxoLLC6oXxJ6ugeEioEF5PYVepmoKZYW7bUE_8nj4nCMvxx939tGOjTFGOAYU0ck_V_TpBMA3fpyk_mbe64ntRMN3K6QNj1YFYLb2ZoH3izCDflKRQJn_kCW4bA9C7l61nOk9xqPaQD) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF49GqQrz6K5vXKbljTZT_HO7JWWwMkBsPNDaaIZVVhNO_KZMGKOf-jtmPpVb-OQ4UX8aQhpWkl0RrXOC0T_B0p6cPKxHzvN_2-2jJI4KhBi2TebwPMsBLGpNCNxgR9MLCMC0VxNvlmsqp3OdRMm4Dr2b0kqTEzJVbi1qU8hLEMQvYVCPQn7rKs2JyxEw==) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx3) [askwoody](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx4) [tips2fix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx5) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHEbdTnxE8OiGPtYeYHIHjI-FYdPFapSsyvEkFQETAn4EGOFBW70zyMuGWQJAODHUXvNkuN-_asN6MPAKjr1s_Snkz91otKTXzErv-XHSEMFHXGIJndiTHDBZdzh-M_K_GknSdGeZ9mAbr1wbKh2TRK9R_59uUy5nQ=). This means older CPUs lacking these instruction sets will not be able to run the update, and the system will hang on boot [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF49GqQrz6K5vXKbljTZT_HO7JWWwMkBsPNDaaIZVVhNO_KZMGKOf-jtmPpVb-OQ4UX8aQhpWkl0RrXOC0T_B0p6cPKxHzvN_2-2jJI4KhBi2TebwPMsBLGpNCNxgR9MLCMC0VxNvlmsqp3OdRMm4Dr2b0kqTEzJVbi1qU8hLEMQvYVCPQn7rKs2JyxEw==).
*   **Performance:** Some reports indicate smoother performance and faster boot times with 24H2 [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR3), with improved FPS in some games [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR4). However, it may have lower app start-up performance and may require a minimum of 32 GB of RAM for optimal performance [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR6).
*   **Known Issues:** 24H2 has a longer list of known issues, including broken biometrics and camera support, and compatibility issues with some older games and applications [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQELURezC4nSeSGTAB1Rn4BCtjuVRX-rbZCkMmoBpyaQlCUog0ZBaBARwr7QfN85XaUyOr4B9YLBwXt2lanV21o6mMilTPmpqRjt2POa7djftDPYzMlB-veZ8ohfTntN26asQ6rRf2vk1NLbzO8en6ae-w==). For example, older games using Easy Anti-Cheat (prior to April 2024) may experience blue screen errors [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGNRMEPE1XyWjBLy5uoFkth6cRXpafQGE3PLBS7PnlCOR0huje8bI_FA4sMK8rgBAYrPfDe7J7yhR6SFxS4o8PCaaviyBk7_aAxxH6AgT3Vs4F7hWjg7dfGfHG2M8sFOSU35cu-9LEnlTMriH9Iulb5SKzStp6QgwLL0sYhtzrt6VMP95V6mfxbh8M9PMRe) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwv_zcA_VFbU7LbmMpY5yi116ibleIdfbvSPXACBK9EgbFgllHdIoMmtovitpwh5zw2q5j0pXg-2ytDJr70JH05MYcoj3LTBEzEBC8Jdfq1lCMaCmD5wFGiij-zHQbRU1uEP_g9wcF9P4s-l9UlMg81cH3wzym9glV4m1rus75m_kegGDm9RMw5Q==).
*   **Security:** Both receive regular security updates [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR4), but upgrading to 24H2 ensures the latest protections [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR4).

**Recommendation for Modern PCs:**

Given that today is June 18, 2025:

*   **If you're on 23H2:** Consider upgrading to 24H2 to receive continued support and the latest features, but be aware of the stricter CPU requirements and potential compatibility issues with older software.  Ensure your system meets the SSE4.2 and POPCNT CPU instruction requirements [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx2) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF9lBOUpt0Su9Ha8-vwby6EmsuVHPmtgIvokFeAD-oLhOe8skcN-wb-MY2ykmCEpHaqh_8DunqsvH3_tX6jHGxoLLC6oXxJ6ugeEioEF5PYVepmoKZYW7bUE_8nj4nCMvxx939tGOjTFGOAYU0ck_V_TpBMA3fpyk_mbe64ntRMN3K6QNj1YFYLb2ZoH3izCDflKRQJn_kCW4bA9C7l61nOk9xqPaQD) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF49GqQrz6K5vXKbljTZT_HO7JWWwMkBsPNDaaIZVVhNO_KZMGKOf-jtmPpVb-OQ4UX8aQhpWkl0RrXOC0T_B0p6cPKxHzvN_2-2jJI4KhBi2TebwPMsBLGpNCNxgR9MLCMC0VxNvlmsqp3OdRMm4Dr2b0kqTEzJVbi1qU8hLEMQvYVCPQn7rKs2JyxEw==) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx3) [askwoody](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx4) [tips2fix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFwYTtJB9V0A5RlrS2VqarV8CStsAhUdpZZgQeWEHn1M1jrOP_f-QXy4_0VqpVJZNjrv9hLH2i2oZKuJ1QKQZsMviZm912kghPi3AicQ0JOj9GIo2jwrMGNgptFk_AfpRRHSz2WdZfaWUzKp-RxdIB4rjhV06fz31WW-Ebx5) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHEbdTnxE8OiGPtYeYHIHjI-FYdPFapSsyvEkFQETAn4EGOFBW70zyMuGWQJAODHUXvNkuN-_asN6MPAKjr1s_Snkz91otKTXzErv-XHSEMFHXGIJndiTHDBZdzh-M_K_GknSdGeZ9mAbr1wbKh2TRK9R_59uUy5nQ=).
*   **If you're on an older version of Windows 11:** Upgrading to either 23H2 or 24H2 is recommended, with 24H2 being the better choice for long-term support, assuming your hardware is compatible.
*   **If you rely on specific older applications or games:** Check for compatibility issues before upgrading to 24H2.
*   **If you're a gamer:** Be aware of potential alt-tab issues with Nvidia GPUs in 24H2.
*   **If security is a top priority:** Upgrading to 24H2 is recommended [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGbEQ-vKHZ_S4KpWTTgOg8wGQdH9kiXL6H9xuslPBFYotKsl7BYVsQ_8M25LvIU84USNAfpmnthNrbJED7UQPRKdzu8aq5ROpSGgGK1yejH1VVOgeb8IhFlgiuC33Lk35MhWuX9ry_vXD1fCWfk6iV9k0kQjGZ6tFH3heaBZKocwz8RCaGI8cgfGAj0yFCbM-AR4).

--- Research Result 1 ---
Windows 11 Insider Preview Build 27813, released to the Canary Channel on March 12, 2025, includes several changes, fixes, and improvements. [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [winaero](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2)

**Key Updates and Changes:**

*   **Removal of Location History:** The Location History feature, an API used by Cortana to access 24 hours of device history when location was enabled, has been removed. [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [winaero](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [itstechbased](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) Consequently, location data will no longer be saved locally, and the corresponding settings have been removed from Settings > Privacy & security > Location page. [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [winaero](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) [itstechbased](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) \[2, 3, 4, 5, 12, 16, 18] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)
*   **Optional Features Settings Page:** The settings app has a new feature. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) In Settings > System > Optional Features, when you click on "View Features," you now have the option to switch between already added features and available features that you can add. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) \[2, 16] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)

**App Updates:**

*   **Snipping Tool:** The snipping tool app has a new feature where you can draw certain shapes and hold your mouse clicked, and those shapes will be generated automatically by the app. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) The snipping tool app is doing a protocol launch for developers. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) App callers can now customize which snipping tool capture features are shown when invoked from their experience. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [itstechbased](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) \[2, 16] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)
*   **Notepad:** Notepad has a new Copilot preview dropdown that allows you to summarize text, but it requires a subscription. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) There is also a new "recent" option under "file" where you can see your recent Notepad apps, and you can clear the list. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) \[2, 16] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)

**Fixes:**

*   **Audio:** Fixed an issue with the WDMAud system driver which was leading to some app crashes after the recent MIDI work. \[2, 3, 4, 5, 12, 16] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)
*   **Settings:** Fixed an issue where in Settings > System > Display > Color Management, it might not display the expected color profile list for the selected monitor. \[2, 3, 4, 5, 12] [logicstechnology](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [softwarekeep](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [xda-developers](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [windows](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)

--- Research Result 2 ---
Here's a comparison of Windows 11 24H2 and 23H2 for modern PCs, based on the provided search results:

**Release Dates and Availability:**

*   **Windows 11 23H2:** Released on October 31, 2023. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3)
*   **Windows 11 24H2:** Initially rolled out for Copilot+ PCs on June 15, 2024, and became generally available to all Windows 11 users on October 1, 2024. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)

**Servicing Timeline:**

*   Windows 11 has an annual feature update cadence, released in the second half of the calendar year. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
*   **23H2:**
    *   Home, Pro, Pro for Workstations, and Pro Education editions are serviced for 24 months from the release date. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) End of service is November 11, 2025. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)
    *   Enterprise and Education editions are serviced for 36 months from the release date. End of service is November 10, 2026.
*   **24H2:**
    *   Home, Pro, Pro Education, and Pro for Workstations editions are serviced for 24 months from the release date. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) End of service is October 13, 2026. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
    *   Enterprise and Education editions are serviced for 36 months from the release date. End of service is October 12, 2027. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
    *   Enterprise LTSC edition will reach end of service on October 9, 2029. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
    *   IoT Enterprise LTSC edition will have extended support until October 10, 2034. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)

**Installation Method:**

*   **23H2:** Shipped as an enablement package for the "Windows 11 2022 Update" (22H2). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5)
*   **24H2:** Installed using the "OS swap" method, replacing the entire OS with a newer version.

**Key Features and Improvements:**

*   **Copilot:**
    *   **23H2:** Replaced Windows Cortana with Windows Copilot, an AI assistant.
    *   **24H2:** Introduces the Windows Copilot PWA (Progressive Web App), which can be moved and snapped like a normal app. [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)
*   **File Explorer:**
    *   **23H2:** Native support for RAR and other file compression formats. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)
    *   **24H2:** Support for creating 7-zip and TAR archives. Text labels added to context menu icons (copy, paste, delete, rename). [tomsguide](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9) Ability to edit metadata of PNG image files. [pcmag](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-10)
*   **Energy Saver:**
    *   **24H2:** Introduces a new "Energy Saver" mode for both PCs with and without batteries, reducing energy consumption by reducing system performance. [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6) [tomsguide](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9)
*   **Phone Link:**
    *   **24H2:** Improvements to phone linking capabilities between Windows and Android devices, including a new "manage mobile devices" app and the ability to set up your phone as a webcam. [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)
*   **Quick Settings:**
    *   **24H2:** Expanded Quick Settings menu with easy access to all tools. [tomsguide](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9)
*   **Taskbar:**
    *   **23H2:** Ability to ungroup icons and show labels on the taskbar.
*   **Other 24H2 Features:**
    *   HDR background support. [pcmag](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-10)
    *   Support for Wi-Fi 7 (802.11be) and Bluetooth LE audio.
    *   Windows Search can search for documents and photos using descriptive phrases. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
    *   Auto Super Resolution (requires a Copilot+ PC with a Snapdragon X processor). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
    *   Windows Recall (preview) to find previously viewed content.
    *   Live Captions to translate audio and video content into English subtitles from 44 languages (Copilot+ PCs). [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)
    *   Cocreator in Paint (Copilot+ PCs). [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)
*   **Other 23H2 Features:**
    *   New volume mixer. [starwindsoftware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-12) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)
    *   Dynamic Lighting and RGB control. [starwindsoftware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-12) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)
    *   Windows Backup was re-introduced with a new look and feature set for Windows 11. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)
    *   Passkey support on the OS level was implemented via the biometric Windows Hello system. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)

**System Requirements:**

*   **24H2:** Introduces modified system requirements: A x86-64-v2 CPU supporting SSE4.2 and POPCNT CPU instructions is now required.

**Performance:**

*   **24H2:** Some reports indicate smoother performance and faster boot times compared to 23H2. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-13)
*   **24H2:** Improved FPS in some games. [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-14)
*   **24H2:** May have lower app start-up performance compared to 23H2.
*   **24H2:** Clean install may result in better scaling with higher processor thread counts. [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-15)
*   **24H2:** May require a minimum of 32 GB of RAM for optimal performance. [neowin](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-16)

**Known Issues:**

*   **24H2:** Has a longer list of known issues, including broken biometrics and camera support on some devices, and compatibility issues with some older games and applications. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)

**Security:**

*   Both 23H2 and 24H2 receive regular security updates. [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-14)
*   Upgrading to 24H2 ensures access to the latest protections. [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-14)

**Upgrade Considerations:**

*   If you are an avid gamer with an Nvidia GPU, be aware of potential alt-tab issues in 24H2.
*   If security is a top priority, upgrading to 24H2 is recommended. [dtptips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-14)
*   If you rely on specific older applications or games, check for compatibility issues before upgrading to 24H2.

--- Research Result 4 ---
Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent information on the "Energy Saver" mode in Windows 11 24H2, focusing on its technical details, performance reduction methods, and impact on various hardware configurations. Then, I will synthesize the findings into a verifiable text artifact.

Here's a consolidated report on the "Energy Saver" mode in Windows 11 24H2, based on the search results:

**Overview:**

*   The "Energy Saver" mode replaces the traditional "Battery Saver" in Windows 11 24H2 and later versions. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) \[2, 3, 16] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   It aims to extend battery life and reduce energy consumption by automatically managing power usage across the system and apps. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) \[2, 3, 16] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Microsoft recommends enabling "Energy Saver" all the time, even when the device has plenty of charge. \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   The feature is available on both laptops and desktop PCs. [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [acer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) \[7, 11, 16, 19] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)

**Technical Details & Functionality:**

*   **Power Management:** "Energy Saver" manages power usage across the system and apps to balance performance and energy efficiency. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) \[2, 16] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **User Interaction-Aware CPU Power Management:** Windows 11 24H2 introduces a "User Interaction-Aware CPU Power Management" feature that reduces energy consumption when the device is not actively in use. \[4, 5, 15] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
    *   It detects inactivity based on mouse, keyboard, or screen input. [ghacks](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) [itdaily](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) \[4]
    *   The CPU is then throttled to lower clock speeds or enters a sleep-like state (C-state). [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) [ghacks](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) \[4, 5, 15] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
    *   Windows restores the CPU to normal speed upon user interaction. [itdaily](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) \[5] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
    *   This feature may be disabled by the user. [itdaily](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) \[4, 15] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **Automatic Activation:** "Energy Saver" can be configured to turn on automatically when the battery reaches a certain percentage. [qts-ltd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [acer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) \[2, 3, 7, 17] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **Manual Activation:** Users can toggle "Energy Saver" on or off via Quick Settings in the system tray. [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **Intune Management:** IT administrators can manage "Energy Saver" settings on Windows 11 PCs through group policies and Mobile Device Management (MDM) configurations via Microsoft Intune. \[16] [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)

**Impact on System Performance:**

*   "Energy Saver" extends battery life at the cost of performance. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) \[9] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   It reduces system performance to lower power consumption. [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12) \[8, 19] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   When "Energy Saver" is active, users cannot change the power mode in Windows Settings. \[2, 3, 11] [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   Display brightness is reduced by 30% by default, but users can enable/disable this setting. [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12) OEMs can configure the default brightness value. \[2, 3, 16] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Transparency effects on window backgrounds are disabled. [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) \[2, 3, 21] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Background apps are blocked from running, although users can allow specific apps to run. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) Certain app categories like VOIP apps are not blocked. [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Certain Microsoft apps (OneNote, OneDrive, Phone Link, etc.) may not sync. \[2, 3, 21] [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   Non-critical Windows Update downloads are blocked, but update scans still occur. [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   The majority of telemetry data uploads are blocked. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [edtittel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Windows Task Scheduler tasks trigger only if the task is not set to start only if the computer is idle. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) \[2, 3] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   CPU and GPU performance may be lowered. \[8] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Some users have reported CPU throttling issues with certain Intel CPUs (e.g., Intel Ultra 9 285K) in Windows 11 24H2, where the system unexpectedly downshifts performance when applications lose focus. [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13) \[13, 14] [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)

**Impact on Different Hardware Configurations:**

*   The impact of "Energy Saver" can vary based on hardware compatibility and clean installation. \[1]
*   AI-powered features like Recall and Click to Do require Copilot+ PCs with NPUs. \[1] [techvertu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-14)

[microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) ([1]) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [elmdaleit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [tomshardware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [ipcamtalk](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [overclock3d](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
*   **Display Resolution:** HD (720p) display greater than 9 inches diagonally, with 8 bits per color channel. **CPU Specific Requirements and Compatibility:**

*   **x86-64-v2 Architecture:** Windows 11 24H2 introduces a modified system requirement: a x86-64-v2 CPU is now required. ([2]) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [elmdaleit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [tomshardware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [ipcamtalk](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [overclock3d](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
*   **SSE4.2 and POPCNT Instructions:** The CPU must support SSE4.2 and POPCNT CPU instructions. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13) [askwoody](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-14) [tips2fix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-15) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) If the CPU lacks these instructions, the Windows kernel will be unbootable. ([2]) This primarily affects systems bypassing the requirements and all 24H2 IoT Enterprise editions. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13) ([2]) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [elmdaleit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [tomshardware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [ipcamtalk](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [overclock3d](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
*   **Implications for CPU Compatibility:** This requirement means that older CPUs lacking these instruction sets will not be able to run the update, and the system will hang on boot. [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) ([4]) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [elmdaleit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [tomshardware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [ipcamtalk](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [overclock3d](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
*   **Supported Processors:**
    *   **Intel:** 8th Gen (Coffee Lake) and newer processors are generally supported, including some Pentium, Atom, Celeron, and Xeon CPUs. ([1], [6]) Some 7th Gen Intel Core chips (specifically the 7820HQ) are also supported. ([1]) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [elevenforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [elmdaleit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [tomshardware](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [ipcamtalk](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [overclock3d](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7) [tenforums](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [superuser](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
    *   **AMD:** 2nd generation Ryzen (including Threadripper) and newer processors are supported, along with some EPYC and Athlon CPUs. ([1]) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
    *   **ARM:** ARMv8.1 is now required for ARM variants, dropping unofficial support for ARMv8. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13)0. ([2]) On ARMv8.0 CPUs, the Windows kernel is unbootable. ([2]) ARM variants drop support for 32-bit ARM applications; only 64-bit ARM applications will run. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13) ([2]) Supported Qualcomm processors include Snapdragon X Elite, Snapdragon X Plus, Snapdragon 850, 7c, 8c, and 8cx (Gen2), and Microsoft SQ1 and SQ2. ([1]) [pureinfotech](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Specific CPU Models:** Microsoft has released lists of supported AMD and Intel processors for Windows 11 24H2. ([3]) These lists are updated periodically. ([8])
*   **Incompatible CPUs:** Systems with CPUs older than those specified (e.g., Core 2 Duo, Phenom II) that do not support SSE4.2 and POPCNT will not be able to boot Windows 11 24H2. ([11], [20])
*   **Bypassing Requirements:** While it was possible to bypass some Windows 11 requirements in the past, the SSE4.2 and POPCNT requirements are "hard" requirements and cannot be bypassed. ([11], [20])

**Additional Notes:**

*   **Copilot+ PCs:** To be considered a Copilot+ PC, the system requires a Snapdragon X, AMD Ryzen AI 300, or Intel Core Ultra 200V series processor, an NPU with 40+ TOPS, 16GB of RAM, and 256GB of SSD storage.
